## below and below'

## Relationship between below and above

<pre class="Agda"><a id="upRight-downLeft-pos"></a><a id="12906" href="TWA.Thesis.Chapter5.BelowAndAbove.html#12906" class="Function">upRight-downLeft-pos</a> <a id="12927" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12929" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12930" href="TWA.Thesis.Chapter5.BelowAndAbove.html#12930" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="12932" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="12934" href="MLTT.Natural-Numbers-Type.html#110" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="12935" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="12937" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="12939" href="Integers.Type.html#792" class="InductiveConstructor">pos</a> <a id="12943" href="TWA.Thesis.Chapter5.BelowAndAbove.html#12930" class="Bound">b</a> <a id="12945" href="MLTT.Id.html#207" class="Datatype Operator">＝</a> <a id="12947" href="TWA.Thesis.Chapter5.BelowAndAbove.html#6825" class="Function">upRight</a> <a id="12955" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12956" href="TWA.Thesis.Chapter5.BelowAndAbove.html#528" class="Function">downLeft</a> <a id="12965" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="12966" href="Integers.Type.html#792" class="InductiveConstructor">pos</a> <a id="12970" href="TWA.Thesis.Chapter5.BelowAndAbove.html#12930" class="Bound">b</a><a id="12971" class="Symbol">))</a>
